var toast = $('#toast').dxToast({ displayTime: 5000, closeOnClick: true, position: 'top center' }).dxToast('instance');
function showToast(type, message) {
  toast.option({ message, type });
  toast.show();
}

const tabs = [
  {
    id: 0,
    text: "EAST",
    inputs: "eastInputs",

const baseurl = ROOT_URL;

let { year, futureMonthName, monthName, shortMonth, shortFutureMonth } = getActiveMonth()
let readMonth = (isPlanningMonth ? shortFutureMonth?.toUpperCase() : shortMonth?.toUpperCase()) + year



function getActiveMonth() {
  let year = moment().format("YYYY");
  let monthName = moment().format("MMMM");
  let futureMonthName = moment().add(1, "month").format("MMMM");
  return { year, futureMonthName, monthName, shortMonth: moment().format("MMM"), shortFutureMonth: moment().add(1, "month").format("MMM") }
}
function setHeaderDate() {
  var planningMonth = (isPlanningMonth ? futureMonthName : monthName) + " " + year;
  $("#datepicker1").html(planningMonth);
}
const viewBtnConfig = [
  {
    icon: 'contentlayout',
    alignment: 'grid',
    hint: 'Grid',
  },
  {
    icon: 'chart',
    alignment: 'chart',
    hint: 'Chart',
  },
]
var isReciptUpdated = false
var today = new Date()
function checkSameDay(d1, d2) {
  return d1.getFullYear() === d2.getFullYear() &&
    d1.getMonth() === d2.getMonth() &&
    d1.getDate() === d2.getDate();
}
function highlightFutureDate(e) {
  if (e.rowType == 'data') {
    let { data } = e;
    let isSameDay = checkSameDay(data?.DATE, today) && data.ROW_COUNT == 1
    if (isSameDay)
      e.rowElement.css({
        "border-top": "2px solid #CCC",
      });
  }
}

$(() => {

  $('#viewBtns').dxButtonGroup({
    items: viewBtnConfig,
    keyExpr: 'alignment',
    stylingMode: 'outlined',
    selectedItemKeys: ['grid'],
    onItemClick: (e) => {
      let { hint } = e.itemData;
      switch (hint) {
        case 'Chart':
          $('#grid').hide()
          $('#chart').show();
          break;

        default:
          $('#grid').show()
          $('#chart').hide()
          break;
      }
    },
  });


  $('#westInputs').hide()
  const regionTabs = $("#region-tabs > .tabs-container")
    .dxTabs({
      dataSource: tabs,
      selectedIndex: 0,
      animationEnabled: true,
      swipeEnabled: true,
      onItemClick(e) {
        regionTabs.option("selectedIndex", e.itemData.id);
        if (e.itemData.text == 'EAST') {
          $('#westInputs').hide();
          $('#eastInputs').show();
        } else {
          $('#eastInputs').hide();
          $('#westInputs').show();
        }

        handleFilter()
      }
    })
    .dxTabs("instance");

  $('#chart').hide()

  setHeaderDate();

  // format mapper
  function formatDateToNumber(dt) {
    return dt ? Number(dt?.trim().substr(0, 2)) : dt
  }
  function mapCellTemplate(cellElement, cellInfo) {
    let isEditable = checkEditable(cellInfo, 'cellTemplate')

    if (isEditable)
      cellElement.css({ 'background': COLORS.yellow })
    cellElement.text((cellInfo?.value)?Math.round(cellInfo?.value): '')
  }

  function mapPercentTemplate(e, data) {
    let { value } = data;
    let { dataField } = data?.column
    let isPropane = dataField == dataFields.PROPANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT
    let regionValue = regionTabs.option("selectedItem");
    let minValue = regionConstants[regionValue?.inputs][isPropane ? 'propane_min' : 'butane_min'].option('value')
    let maxValue = regionConstants[regionValue?.inputs][isPropane ? 'propane_max' : 'butane_max'].option('value')
    let isAlert = value < minValue || value > maxValue;
    let actValue = Math.round(data?.value)
    var percentageValue = Math.min(actValue, 100);
    if (data?.value) {
      let txt = actValue ? actValue + "%" : null;
      e.html(`<div class="progress" style="position:relative; background: rgb(89 89 89 / 60%);"  >
      <div class="progress-bar" role="progressbar" style="width: ${percentageValue}%;
      background: ${isAlert ? COLORS.error : isPropane ? COLORS.progrss_color_proane : COLORS.progrss_color_butane};

       " aria-valuenow="25" aria-valuemin="0" aria-valuemax="100"> <span style="position:absolute; z-index:2"  >${txt} </span> </div>
    </div>`
      )
    }
    return e

  }

  // Grid code
  getData();
  function getChartData(list) {
    let newData = list?.filter(obj => {
      let { REGION, ROW_COUNT } = obj || {}
      const isValid = REGION == regionTabs.option("selectedItem")?.text && ROW_COUNT == 1;
      return isValid
    });
    return newData
  }

  function handleFilter() {
    let params = {
      Region: regionTabs.option("selectedItem")?.text,
    }

    let ADJUSTMENT = getChartData(adjustmentGrid.option('dataSource'))
    projectionGrid.filter(function (itemData) {
      let { REGION, ROW_COUNT } = itemData || {}
      let finder = REGION == params.Region;
      return finder;
    })
    adjustmentGrid.filter(function (itemData) {
      let { REGION } = itemData || {}
      let finder = REGION == params.Region;
      return finder;
    });

    // Graph
    propaneChart.option('dataSource', ADJUSTMENT);
    butaneChart.option('dataSource', ADJUSTMENT);
    maxinventoryPerc = Math.max(100, ADJUSTMENT.BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT, ADJUSTMENT.PROPANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT);
    propaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].visualRange[0]`, [0, maxinventoryPerc]);
    butaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].visualRange[0]`, [0, maxinventoryPerc]);
    propaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].visualRange[1]`, [0, maxinventoryPerc]);
    butaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].visualRange[1]`, [0, maxinventoryPerc]);
    let inputs = params.Region == 'EAST' ? eastInputs : westInputs;

    // update min-max values in chart
    updateConstLines(true, 'propane', inputs.propane_min.option('value'))
    updateConstLines(true, 'butane', inputs.butane_min.option('value'))
    updateConstLines(false, 'propane', inputs.propane_max.option('value'))
    updateConstLines(false, 'butane', inputs.butane_max.option('value'))
  }
  function setInputConstants(resp, i) {
    let key = i == 0 ? 'eastInputs' : 'westInputs';

    regionConstants?.[key].working_capacity_propane.option('value', resp?.WORKING_CAPACITY?.[i].WORKING_CAPACITY_PROPANE)
    regionConstants?.[key]?.working_capacity_butane.option('value', resp?.WORKING_CAPACITY?.[i].WORKING_CAPACITY_BUTANE)

    regionConstants?.[key]?.adjust_capacity_propane.option('value', resp?.ADJUSTED_CAPACITY?.[i].ADJUSTED_CAPACITY_PROPANE)
    regionConstants?.[key]?.adjust_capacity_butane.option('value', resp?.ADJUSTED_CAPACITY?.[i].ADJUSTED_CAPACITY_BUTANE)

    regionConstants?.[key]?.propane_min.option('value', resp?.MIN?.[i].MIN_PROPANE)
    regionConstants?.[key]?.butane_min.option('value', resp?.MIN?.[i].MIN_BUTANE)
    regionConstants?.[key]?.propane_max.option('value', resp?.MAX?.[i].MAX_PROPANE)
    regionConstants?.[key]?.butane_max.option('value', resp?.MAX?.[i].MAX_BUTANE)
  }

  function calcPercent({ obj, i, arr }, gridKey) {
    let newObj = { ...obj }
    let { OPENING_INV_PROPANE, OPENING_INV_BUTANE, ROW_COUNT } = obj;
    if (ROW_COUNT == 2)
      return;

    let regionObj = regionTabs.option("selectedItem");
    let isEast = regionObj?.text == 'EAST';

    let key = regionObj?.inputs;
    let wk_cap_propane = regionConstants?.[key].working_capacity_propane.option('value');
    let wk_cap_butane = regionConstants?.[key].working_capacity_butane.option('value');


    if (gridKey == 'ADJUSTMENT' || gridKey == 'ADJUSTMENT-updateGridPercent' ) {
      let DATE = new Date((obj?.NOMINATION_EFFECTIVE_DT).trim().substr(0, 9))
      let DAY = new Date((obj?.NOMINATION_EFFECTIVE_DT).trim().substr(0, 9)).getDate()
      let MONTH = new Date((obj?.NOMINATION_EFFECTIVE_DT).trim().substr(0, 9)).getMonth()
      let DAYMONTH = (obj?.NOMINATION_EFFECTIVE_DT).trim().substr(0, 5)
      let prevNonEmptyRowIndex = i - (arr[i - 1])?.ROW_COUNT || 0 ;
      if (DATE < today) {
        newObj.CLOSING_ADJ_INV_PROPANE = obj?.CLOSING_INV_PROPANE;// propane
        newObj.CLOSING_ADJ_INV_BUTANE = obj?.CLOSING_INV_BUTANE;

        newObj.PROPANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT = (obj?.CLOSING_INV_PROPANE / wk_cap_propane * 100);
        newObj.BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT = (obj?.CLOSING_INV_BUTANE / wk_cap_butane * 100);
      }
      else {
        let { closingInvPercent, adjInventory } = calcInventoryBykey({
          CLOSING_INV: obj?.CLOSING_INV_PROPANE, TERMINAL_RECEIPT: obj?.TERMINAL_RECEIPT_PROPANE, CUST_LIFTING: obj?.CUST_LIFTING_PROPANE,
          ACT_TERM_RECEIPT: obj?.ACT_TERM_RECEIPT_PROPANE,
          ACT_CUST_LIFTING: obj?.ACT_CUST_LIFTING_PROPANE,
          ROW_ORDER: obj?.ROW_ORDER,
          ROW_COUNT: obj?.ROW_COUNT,
          DAY,
          MONTH,
          DATE,
          DAYMONTH,
          LIFTING_VALUE: (arr?.[i + 1]?.CUST_LIFTING_PROPANE || 0),
          PREV_CLOSING_ADJ_INV: (arr[prevNonEmptyRowIndex]?.CLOSING_ADJ_INV_PROPANE || 0)
        }, 'CUST_LIFTING_PROPANE');

        let { closingInvPercent: closingInvPercentButane, adjInventory: adjInventoryButane } = calcInventoryBykey({
          CLOSING_INV: obj?.CLOSING_INV_BUTANE, TERMINAL_RECEIPT: obj?.TERMINAL_RECEIPT_BUTANE,
          ACT_TERM_RECEIPT: obj?.ACT_TERM_RECEIPT_BUTANE,
          ACT_CUST_LIFTING: obj?.ACT_CUST_LIFTING_BUTANE,
          CUST_LIFTING: obj?.CUST_LIFTING_BUTANE,
          ROW_ORDER: obj?.ROW_ORDER,
          DAY,
          MONTH,
          DATE,
          DAYMONTH,
          LIFTING_VALUE: (arr?.[i + 1]?.CUST_LIFTING_BUTANE || 0),
          ROW_COUNT: obj?.ROW_COUNT, PREV_CLOSING_ADJ_INV: (arr[prevNonEmptyRowIndex]?.CLOSING_ADJ_INV_BUTANE || 0)
        }, 'CUST_LIFTING_BUTANE');

        if(gridKey != 'ADJUSTMENT-updateGridPercent') {
          newObj.CLOSING_ADJ_INV_PROPANE = adjInventory;// propane
          newObj.CLOSING_ADJ_INV_BUTANE = adjInventoryButane;

        }

        newObj.PROPANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT = closingInvPercent // propane
        newObj.BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT = closingInvPercentButane;
      }
    }

    if (gridKey != 'ADJUSTMENT') {
      newObj.PROPANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT = (obj?.CLOSING_INV_PROPANE / wk_cap_propane * 100);
      newObj.BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT = (obj?.CLOSING_INV_BUTANE / wk_cap_butane * 100);
    }

    newObj.PROPANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT_ACTUAL = (obj?.CLOSING_INV_PROPANE / wk_cap_propane * 100);
    newObj.BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT_ACTUAL = (obj?.CLOSING_INV_BUTANE / wk_cap_butane * 100);

    // to calculate adjustment closing inventory at page load, for adjustment grid only
    return newObj
  }

  function mapResp(list, key) {
    if (list?.length) {
      list = list?.map((obj, i, arr) => {
        let { NOMINATION_EFFECTIVE_DT } = obj;

        // if row is greater than 2 (1 for west ),opening inventory = prev row opening inv.
        let newObj = { ...obj };
        var percentMapped = calcPercent({ obj, i, arr }, key);

        newObj = { ...newObj, ...percentMapped }
        newObj.DAY = new Date((NOMINATION_EFFECTIVE_DT).trim().substr(0, 9)).getDate();
        newObj.MONTH = new Date((NOMINATION_EFFECTIVE_DT).trim().substr(0, 9)).getMonth();
        newObj.DATE = new Date((NOMINATION_EFFECTIVE_DT).trim().substr(0, 9));
        newObj.DAYMONTH = (NOMINATION_EFFECTIVE_DT).trim().substr(0, 5);

        return arr[i] = newObj
      });
    }
    return list;
  }
  function handleUserGroup({ USER_NM }) {
    user_nm = USER_NM[0];
    getUserDetails(user_nm)
    if (cosmdGroupAccess != -1) {
      reset_Stock();
    }
  }
  function handleResp(resp) {
    let { WORKING_CAPACITY, MIN, MAX, USER_NM } = resp;
    let ACTUAL_FROM_STOCK_PROJ = resp?.ACTUAL_FROM_STOCK_PROJ || [];
    let ADJUSTMENT = resp?.ADJUSTMENT || []

    // input constants values;
    setInputConstants(resp, 0)
    setInputConstants(resp, 1)

    ADJUSTMENT = mapResp(ADJUSTMENT, 'ADJUSTMENT')
    ACTUAL_FROM_STOCK_PROJ = mapResp(ACTUAL_FROM_STOCK_PROJ, 'ACTUAL_FROM_STOCK_PROJ')

    projectionGrid.option('dataSource', ACTUAL_FROM_STOCK_PROJ);
    adjustmentGrid.option('dataSource', ADJUSTMENT);

    let lastUpdatedTime = resp?.["_LAST_UPDATED_"][0]?.OPE_MONTH_INV_SIM_UPDATED_DTTM;
    lastUpdatedTime && ($('#lastSaveDate').text(lastUpdatedTime))

    handleFilter();
    handleUserGroup({ USER_NM })

  }
  function handleUpdateAdjustGrid(data) {
    let ADJUSTMENT = mapResp(data?.ADJUSTMENT, 'ADJUSTMENT');
    adjustmentGrid.option('dataSource', ADJUSTMENT);
    handleFilter()

  }
  async function getData() {
    try {
      let url = getDataUrl
      let resp = await sendRequest(`${url}`, "GET");
      response = resp;
      handleResp(resp)


    } catch (err) {
      $('.overlay').hide();
      isTesting && handleResp(response) // testings
    }

  }

    editing: {

      }
    ],
  }).dxDataGrid("instance");

  var inputProps = {
    working_capacity_propane: "",
    adjust_capacity_propane: "",
    working_capacity_butane: "",
    adjust_capacity_butane: "",
    propane_min: "",
    propane_max: "",
    butane_min: "",
    butane_max: ""
  };
  var regionConstants = {
    eastInputs: { ...inputProps },
    westInputs: { ...inputProps },
  }
  var { eastInputs, westInputs } = regionConstants;


  const inputConfig = {
    height: 24,
    width: '4em',
  }

  function updateGridPercent() {
    let ADJUSTMENT = adjustmentGrid.option('dataSource');
    if (ADJUSTMENT?.length) {
      let newAdj = mapResp(ADJUSTMENT, 'ADJUSTMENT-updateGridPercent');
      adjustmentGrid.option('dataSource', newAdj);
      let chartData = getChartData(newAdj);
      propaneChart.option('dataSource', chartData);
      butaneChart.option('dataSource', chartData);
      maxinventoryPerc = Math.max(100, chartData.BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT, chartData.PROPANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT);
      propaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].visualRange[0]`, [0, maxinventoryPerc]);
      butaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].visualRange[0]`, [0, maxinventoryPerc]);
      propaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].visualRange[1]`, [0, maxinventoryPerc]);
      butaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].visualRange[1]`, [0, maxinventoryPerc]);
      let ACTUAL_FROM_STOCK_PROJ = projectionGrid.option('dataSource');
      let newProj = mapResp(ACTUAL_FROM_STOCK_PROJ, 'ACTUAL_FROM_STOCK_PROJ');
      projectionGrid.option('dataSource', newProj);

    }
  }

  for (const key in regionConstants) {
    if (Object.hasOwnProperty.call(regionConstants, key)) {
      const inputs = regionConstants[key];

      inputs.working_capacity_propane = $(`#${key} #working_capacity_propane`).dxNumberBox({
        ...inputConfig,
        disabled: true,
      }).dxNumberBox("instance")
      inputs.working_capacity_butane = $(`#${key} #working_capacity_butane`).dxNumberBox({
        ...inputConfig,
        disabled: true,
      }).dxNumberBox("instance")
      function adjust_onchange(data, prefix) {
        let { WORKING_CAPACITY } = response
        let region = regionTabs.option("selectedItem")?.text
        let wcp = WORKING_CAPACITY?.[region == 'EAST' ? 1 : 1]?.[`WORKING_CAPACITY_${prefix}`]
        inputs[`working_capacity_${prefix?.toLowerCase()}`].option('value', wcp + (+data?.value));
        updateGridPercent()
      }

      inputs.adjust_capacity_propane = $(`#${key} #adjust_capacity_propane`).dxNumberBox({
        ...inputConfig,
        onValueChanged: (data) => adjust_onchange(data, 'PROPANE')

      }).dxNumberBox("instance")

      inputs.adjust_capacity_butane = $(`#${key} #adjust_capacity_butane`).dxNumberBox({
        ...inputConfig,
        onValueChanged: (data) => adjust_onchange(data, 'BUTANE')
      }).dxNumberBox("instance")

      inputs.propane_min = $(`#${key} #propane_min`).dxNumberBox({
        ...inputConfig,
        onValueChanged(data) {
          updateConstLines(true, 'propane', data?.value)
          projectionGrid.refresh() // update grid, highlight min-max value.
          adjustmentGrid.refresh() // update grid, highlight min-max value.

        },
      }).dxNumberBox("instance")
      inputs.butane_min = $(`#${key} #butane_min`).dxNumberBox({
        ...inputConfig,
        onValueChanged(data) {
          updateConstLines(true, 'butane', data?.value)
          projectionGrid.refresh() // update grid, highlight min-max value.
          adjustmentGrid.refresh() // update grid, highlight min-max value.
        },
      }).dxNumberBox("instance")
      inputs.propane_max = $(`#${key} #propane_max`).dxNumberBox({
        ...inputConfig,
        onValueChanged(data) {
          updateConstLines(false, 'propane', data?.value);
          projectionGrid.refresh() // update grid, highlight min-max value.
          adjustmentGrid.refresh() // update grid, highlight min-max value.

        },
      }).dxNumberBox("instance")
      inputs.butane_max = $(`#${key} #butane_max`).dxNumberBox({
        ...inputConfig,
        onValueChanged(data) {
          updateConstLines(false, 'butane', data?.value);
          projectionGrid.refresh() // update grid, highlight min-max value.
          adjustmentGrid.refresh() // update grid, highlight min-max value.

        },
      }).dxNumberBox("instance")

    }
  }

  // min-max value updater in chart
  function updateConstLines(isMin, chart, value) {
    function updateByChart(i) {
      if (chart == 'propane') {
        propaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].constantLines[${i}].value`, value);
        propaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].visualRange[${i}]`, [0, maxinventoryPerc]);

      } else {
        butaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].constantLines[${i}].value`, value);
        butaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].visualRange[${i}]`, [0, maxinventoryPerc]);
      }
    }
    if (isMin) {
      updateByChart(1)
    } else {
      updateByChart(0)
    }
  }
  // common field in both chart
  function getValueAxis(label) {
    // let name = regionTabsValue == 'EAST' ? 'butaneGraph';
    let name = label == 'propane' ? 'PropaneGraph' : 'butaneGraph';
    return [{
      name,
      position: 'left',
      visualRange: [0, maxinventoryPerc],
      visualRangeUpdateMode: 'keep',
      title: '',
      constantLines: [
        {
          value: 80, width: 2,
          color: 'red',
          dashStyle: 'solid', label: {
            visible: true,
            text: 'Safe Max'
          }
        },
        {
          value: 20, width: 2,
          color: 'red',
          dashStyle: 'solid', label: {
            visible: true,
            text: 'Safe Min'
          }
        }]
    },]


  }



  var butaneChart = $("#butaneChart").dxChart({
    palette: 'Harmony Light',
    size: {
      width: "100%",
    },
    title: {
      text: 'Butane Closing Inventory %',
      font: {
        color: COLORS.g_blue,
        size: 18,
        weight: 600
      }
    },
    valueAxis: getValueAxis('butane'),
    commonSeriesSettings: {
      argumentField: 'DAYMONTH',
      point: {
        visible: false
      }
    },
    series:
      [
        {
          type: 'line',
          valueField: 'BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT',
          axis: 'butaneGraph',
          name: 'Adjusted Inventory',
          color: COLORS.g_yellow,
        },
        {
          type: 'line',
          valueField: 'BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT_ACTUAL',
          axis: 'butaneGraph',
          name: 'Actual Inventory',
          color: COLORS.g_blue,
        },
      ]
    ,
    tooltip: {
      enabled: true,
      location: "edge",
      customizeTooltip: function (arg) {
        return {
          text: "Day: " + arg.argument + "<br/>" + arg.seriesName + ": " + Math.round(arg.valueText)
        };
      },
    },
    argumentAxis: {
      tickInterval: 1
    },
    legend: {
      verticalAlignment: 'bottom',
      horizontalAlignment: 'center',
    },


  }).dxChart("instance");

  setTimeout(function () {
    butaneChart.render();
    propaneChart.render();
  }, 100);


  function calcInventoryBykey(config, key) {
    let { CLOSING_INV, TERMINAL_RECEIPT, CUST_LIFTING,
      LIFTING_VALUE,
      PREV_CLOSING_ADJ_INV,
      ACT_TERM_RECEIPT,
      ACT_CUST_LIFTING,
      DAY,
      MONTH,
      DATE,
      DAYMONTH,
    } = config;
    let prefix = key?.includes('PROPANE') ? 'PROPANE' : 'BUTANE';
    let isNextDate = DATE >= today;
    if (isNextDate) {
      let RHSClosinginv = PREV_CLOSING_ADJ_INV, LHSReceipt = ACT_TERM_RECEIPT, LHSLifting = ACT_CUST_LIFTING;
      // RHS Closing inv. of the previous day + LHS Receipt  LHS Lifting
      CLOSING_INV = (RHSClosinginv || 0) + (LHSReceipt || 0) - (LHSLifting || 0);
    }
    let adjInventory = +(CLOSING_INV || 0) + +(TERMINAL_RECEIPT || 0) - +(CUST_LIFTING || 0) - (LIFTING_VALUE || 0);
    const inputs = regionTabs.option("selectedItem")?.inputs;
    let wk_cap_propane = regionConstants[inputs][`working_capacity_${prefix.toLowerCase()}`].option('value')
    let closingInvPercent = +adjInventory / wk_cap_propane * 100;

    return { adjInventory: adjInventory || null, closingInvPercent: Math.round(closingInvPercent) || null }
  }
  function checkEditable(e, key) {
    let dt = e.row.data.NOMINATION_EFFECTIVE_DT;
    // let DATE = new Date((e.row.data.NOMINATION_EFFECTIVE_DT).trim().substr(0, 9));
    let { ROW_COUNT, DATE } = e?.row?.data || {}
    let dataField = e?.column?.dataField
    let isEditable = false;
    // enable editing for date greater than today
    if (dt) {
      dt = formatDateToNumber(dt)
      let today = new Date();
      let isEmptyRecipt = ROW_COUNT == 2 && (dataField == 'TERMINAL_RECEIPT_BUTANE' || dataField == 'TERMINAL_RECEIPT_PROPANE');
      let isSameDay = checkSameDay(DATE, today)
      isEditable = !isEmptyRecipt && (DATE > today || isSameDay );
    }
    return isEditable
  }
  var adjustmentGrid = $("#gridAdjustment")
    .dxDataGrid({
      rowAlternationEnabled: true,
      keyExpr: ["ROW_COUNT", "ROW_ORDER"],
      showBorders: true,
      // columnAutoWidth: true,
      selection: {
        caption: "Select All",
        allowSelectAll: false,
        showCheckBoxesMode: "always",
        mode: "multiple"
      },

      onContentReady(e) {
        let activeScrollContainer = e.component.getScrollable();
        setTimeout(() => {
          activeScrollContainer.on("scroll", () => {
            let activeTop = activeScrollContainer.scrollTop();
            let targetTop = $("#gridProjection").dxDataGrid("instance").getScrollable();

            if (activeTop != targetTop) {
              $("#gridProjection").dxDataGrid("instance").getScrollable().scrollTo({
                y: activeScrollContainer.scrollTop(),
              });
            }

          })
        }, 1000)
      },
      onCellPrepared: function (e) {
        if (e.rowType == "header") {
          e.cellElement.css("text-align", "center");
          e.cellElement.css("color", "#fff");
          e.cellElement.css("background-color", "#00A3E0");
          if (e?.column?.type == "selection") {
            e.cellElement.html('SPOT /<br>Additional')
            e.cellElement.css({ fontSize: '0.8em' })
          }
        }
        if (e.rowType == "data") {
          let { FLAG } = e?.data;

          let shouldHide = e.data.DATE < new Date() || (FLAG ? [7, 8, 6]?.includes(FLAG) : false);
          // hide checkbox for old days
          if (e?.columnIndex == 0 && e.column.type == "selection" && shouldHide) {
            e.cellElement.off();
            $(e.cellElement).find('.dx-checkbox').css("display", "none")

          }
          // tick spot rows
          if (e?.columnIndex == 0 && e.column.type == "selection" && FLAG == 9) {

            $(e.cellElement).find('.dx-checkbox').addClass("dx-checkbox-checked");
            $(e.cellElement).find('.dx-checkbox input').prop("value", true)

          }

          e.cellElement.css("text-align", "center");

          let dataField = e.column.dataField;
          // highlight spot
          let isLifting = dataField == 'CUST_LIFTING_PROPANE' || dataField == 'CUST_LIFTING_BUTANE';
          if (isLifting && FLAG) {
            e.cellElement.css({ 'background': suggestionFlags[FLAG] })
          }

        }
      },

      editing: {
        mode: "cell",
        allowUpdating: (e) => checkEditable(e, 'allowUpdate')
      },
      scrolling: {
        useNative: false,
        scrollByContent: true,
        scrollByThumb: true,
        showScrollbar: "onHover" // or "onScroll" | "always" | "never"
      },
      paging: { enabled: false },
      onOptionChanged: function (e) {
        let isPropaneUpdate = e.value?.[0]?.data?.hasOwnProperty('CLOSING_ADJ_INV_PROPANE') && e.value?.[0]?.data?.hasOwnProperty('PROPANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT');
        let isButaneUpdate = e.value?.[0]?.data?.hasOwnProperty('CLOSING_ADJ_INV_BUTANE') && e.value?.[0]?.data?.hasOwnProperty('BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT');
        let prefix = isPropaneUpdate ? 'PROPANE' : 'BUTANE';
        // detect that TERMINAL_RECEIPT_ / Avail value is updated
        isReciptUpdated = isReciptUpdated || e.value?.[0]?.data?.hasOwnProperty(`TERMINAL_RECEIPT_PROPANE`) || e.value?.[0]?.data?.hasOwnProperty(`TERMINAL_RECEIPT_BUTANE`);

        if (isButaneUpdate || isPropaneUpdate) {
          let regionObj = regionTabs.option("selectedItem");
          let isEast = regionObj?.text == 'EAST';
          let { data, key } = e.value?.[0];
          let { ROW_ORDER } = key;
          let adjustSource = e.component.option('dataSource');
          let index = adjustSource.findIndex(obj => obj?.ROW_ORDER == ROW_ORDER);
          adjustSource[index][`CLOSING_ADJ_INV_${prefix}`] = data[`CLOSING_ADJ_INV_${prefix}`];
          adjustSource[index][`${prefix}_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT`] = data[`${prefix}_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT`];
          let updatedValue = adjustSource[index][`TERMINAL_RECEIPT_${prefix}`];
          for (let i = index + 1; i < adjustSource.length; i++) {
            const item = adjustSource[i];
            if (item?.ROW_COUNT !== 2 && item?.REGION == regionObj?.text) {
              let LIFTING_VALUE = isEast ?
                i + 1 < adjustSource.length ?
                  adjustSource[i + 1][`CUST_LIFTING_${prefix}`] : 0
                : 0;//empty row lift value
              let { DATE, DAYMONTH, MONTH, DAY } = item;
              let preNonEmptyRowData =  adjustSource[i - adjustSource[i - 1]?.ROW_COUNT]
              let { adjInventory, closingInvPercent } = calcInventoryBykey({
                CLOSING_INV: item[`CLOSING_INV_${prefix}`],
                TERMINAL_RECEIPT: updatedValue,
                ACT_TERM_RECEIPT: item[`ACT_TERM_RECEIPT_${prefix}`],
                ACT_CUST_LIFTING: item[`ACT_CUST_LIFTING_${prefix}`],
                PREV_CLOSING_ADJ_INV: preNonEmptyRowData[`CLOSING_ADJ_INV_${prefix}`],
                CUST_LIFTING: item[`CUST_LIFTING_${prefix}`],
                LIFTING_VALUE,
                DATE,
                DAYMONTH,
                MONTH,
                DAY
              }, `onOptionChanged-${prefix}`)

              adjustSource[i][`CLOSING_ADJ_INV_${prefix}`] = adjInventory
              adjustSource[i][`${prefix}_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT`] = closingInvPercent;

              // Fill empty values
              adjustSource[i][`TERMINAL_RECEIPT_${prefix}`] = updatedValue
              // if(isReciptUpdated) // later user
            }

          }
          isReciptUpdated = false;
          e.component.option('dataSource', adjustSource)


          // chart sync with grid
          let chartData = getChartData(adjustSource)
          maxinventoryPerc = Math.max(100, chartData.BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT, chartData.PROPANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT);
          propaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].visualRange[0]`, [0, maxinventoryPerc]);
          butaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].visualRange[0]`, [0, maxinventoryPerc]);
          propaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].visualRange[1]`, [0, maxinventoryPerc]);
          butaneChart.option(`valueAxis[0].visualRange[1]`, [0, maxinventoryPerc]);
          propaneChart.option('dataSource', chartData)
          butaneChart.option('dataSource', chartData)

        }
      },
      onRowUpdated: async function (e) {
        // update graph when grid data updated
        let { ROW_ORDER, ROW_COUNT, DATE, DAY, MONTH, DAYMONTH } = e?.data;
        const editColumnName = e.component.option("editing.editColumnName");
        let regionObj = regionTabs.option("selectedItem");
        let isEast = regionObj?.text == 'EAST';

        let isInventoryCalculation = [
          'TERMINAL_RECEIPT_BUTANE', 'CUST_LIFTING_PROPANE',
          'TERMINAL_RECEIPT_PROPANE', 'CUST_LIFTING_BUTANE',
        ].includes(editColumnName)

        if (isInventoryCalculation) {
          let prefix = editColumnName?.includes('PROPANE') ? 'PROPANE' : 'BUTANE';
          let prevNonEmptyKey = { ROW_ORDER: ROW_ORDER - ROW_COUNT - (isEast ? 0 : 0), ROW_COUNT: 1 }

          let preNonEmptyRowData = await e.component.byKey(prevNonEmptyKey);
          let prevKey = { ROW_ORDER: (e?.key?.ROW_ORDER - 1), ROW_COUNT: 1 };
          let activeKey = { ROW_ORDER, ROW_COUNT };
          let isEmptyRow = ROW_COUNT == 2
          let prevIndex = e.component.getRowIndexByKey(prevKey)
          let activeIndex = e.component.getRowIndexByKey(activeKey)



          let calcObj = e?.data
          if (isEmptyRow) {
            calcObj = await e.component.byKey(prevKey);
          }
          let invPayload = {
            CLOSING_INV: calcObj?.[`CLOSING_INV_${prefix}`],
            TERMINAL_RECEIPT: calcObj?.[`TERMINAL_RECEIPT_${prefix}`],
            ACT_TERM_RECEIPT: calcObj?.[`ACT_TERM_RECEIPT_${prefix}`],
            ACT_CUST_LIFTING: calcObj?.[`ACT_CUST_LIFTING_${prefix}`],
            PREV_CLOSING_ADJ_INV: preNonEmptyRowData[`CLOSING_ADJ_INV_${prefix}`],
            CUST_LIFTING: calcObj?.[`CUST_LIFTING_${prefix}`],
            DAY,
            MONTH,
            DATE,
            DAYMONTH,
            LIFTING_VALUE: 0
          };

          if (isEmptyRow) {
            invPayload = {
              ...invPayload,
              LIFTING_VALUE: e?.data?.[`CUST_LIFTING_${prefix}`]

            }
          }


          let { adjInventory, closingInvPercent } = calcInventoryBykey(invPayload, 'CUST_LIFTING_PROPANE_EMPTY')

          let cellIndex = isEmptyRow ? prevIndex : activeIndex;

          e.component.cellValue(cellIndex, `CLOSING_ADJ_INV_${prefix}`, adjInventory);
          e.component.cellValue(cellIndex, `${prefix}_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT`, closingInvPercent);
          getValueAxis("propane");
        }

      },
      onRowPrepared: function (e) {
        // Check if the row index is divisible by 2 (every two rows)
        highlightFutureDate(e)

      },
      onEditorPreparing: function (e) {
        const { dataField } = e || {};
        const { ROW_COUNT } = e?.row?.data || {};
        if (dataField) {
          let isEmptyRecipt = (dataField == 'TERMINAL_RECEIPT_PROPANE' || dataField == 'TERMINAL_RECEIPT_BUTANE') && ROW_COUNT == 2;
          if (dataField === "OPENING_INV_PROPANE" || dataField === "OPENING_INV_BUTANE" || isEmptyRecipt) {
            e.editorOptions.disabled = true;
          }
        }

      },
      onSelectionChanged(selectedItems) {
        let { currentDeselectedRowKeys, currentSelectedRowKeys, selectedRowKeys, selectedRowsData } = selectedItems
        selectedSpotRows = selectedRowsData;

        adjustmentGrid.beginUpdate();
        currentSelectedRowKeys?.forEach(obj => {
          let rowIndex = adjustmentGrid.getRowIndexByKey(obj)
          adjustmentGrid.cellValue(rowIndex, "FLAG", 9);
        })
        currentDeselectedRowKeys?.forEach(obj => {
          let rowIndex = adjustmentGrid.getRowIndexByKey(obj)
          adjustmentGrid.cellValue(rowIndex, "FLAG", 0);
        })
        adjustmentGrid.saveEditData();
        adjustmentGrid.endUpdate();
      },
      columns: [
        { type: "selection" },
        {
          dataField: 'FLAG',
          visible: false
        },
        {
          caption: "Avails",
          columns: [
            {
              caption: "Propane",
              dataField: "TERMINAL_RECEIPT_PROPANE",
              cellTemplate: mapCellTemplate,
              format: { type: "fixedPoint", precision: 0 },

            },
            {
              caption: "Butane",
              dataField: "TERMINAL_RECEIPT_BUTANE",
              cellTemplate: mapCellTemplate,
              format: { type: "fixedPoint", precision: 0 },

            }
          ]
        },
        {
          caption: "Liftings (MB)",
          columns: [
            {
              caption: "Propane",
              dataField: "CUST_LIFTING_PROPANE",
              // showEditorAlways: true,
              cellTemplate: mapCellTemplate,
              format: { type: "fixedPoint", precision: 0 },
            },
            {
              caption: "Butane",
              dataField: "CUST_LIFTING_BUTANE",
              cellTemplate: mapCellTemplate,
              format: { type: "fixedPoint", precision: 0 },
            }
          ]
        },
        {
          caption: "Inventory",
          allowEditing: false,
          columns: [
            {
              caption: "Propane",
              allowEditing: false,
              dataField: "CLOSING_ADJ_INV_PROPANE",
              format: { type: "fixedPoint", precision: 0 },
              calculateDisplayValue: function (rowData) {
                let { CLOSING_INV_PROPANE, CLOSING_ADJ_INV_PROPANE } = rowData
                return CLOSING_ADJ_INV_PROPANE || CLOSING_INV_PROPANE;
              },
            },
            {
              caption: "Butane",
              allowEditing: false,
              dataField: "CLOSING_ADJ_INV_BUTANE",
              format: { type: "fixedPoint", precision: 0 },
              calculateDisplayValue: function (rowData) {
                let { CLOSING_INV_BUTANE, CLOSING_ADJ_INV_BUTANE } = rowData
                return CLOSING_ADJ_INV_BUTANE || CLOSING_INV_BUTANE;
              },
            }
          ]
        },
        {
          caption: "%",
          columns: [
            {
              dataField: "PROPANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT",
              caption: "Propane",
              allowReordering: false,
              allowEditing: false,
              cellTemplate: mapPercentTemplate,
            },
            {
              dataField: "BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT",
              caption: "Butane",
              allowReordering: false,
              allowEditing: false,
              cellTemplate: mapPercentTemplate,

            }
          ]
        }
      ],
    }).dxDataGrid("instance");

  function reset_Stock() {
    let dataSource = adjustmentGrid.option('dataSource');
    let stockDataSource = projectionGrid.option('dataSource');
    dataSource = dataSource?.map(obj => {
      let stockRow = stockDataSource.find(stockObj => stockObj?.ROW_ORDER == obj?.ROW_ORDER)

      return {
        ...obj,
        TERMINAL_RECEIPT_BUTANE: null,
        TERMINAL_RECEIPT_PROPANE: null,
        CUST_LIFTING_BUTANE: null,
        CUST_LIFTING_PROPANE: null,
        CLOSING_ADJ_INV_PROPANE: stockRow?.CLOSING_INV_PROPANE,
        CLOSING_ADJ_INV_BUTANE: stockRow?.CLOSING_INV_BUTANE,
        PROPANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT: stockRow?.PROPANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT,
        BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT: stockRow?.BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT,
        BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT: stockRow?.BUTANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT,
        FLAG: "0",
      }
    });

    adjustmentGrid.option('dataSource', dataSource);

    // reset adjust capasity
    var { eastInputs, westInputs } = regionConstants;
    eastInputs?.adjust_capacity_propane.option('value', 0);
    eastInputs?.adjust_capacity_butane.option('value', 0);
    westInputs?.adjust_capacity_propane.option('value', 0);
    westInputs?.adjust_capacity_butane.option('value', 0);

    // uncheck spot rows
    uncheckAdjustGrid();

  };

  function uncheckAdjustGrid() {
    let selectedKeys = adjustmentGrid.getSelectedRowKeys();
    adjustmentGrid.deselectRows(selectedKeys);
  }

        weight: 600
      }
    },
    valueAxis: getValueAxis('propane'),
    commonSeriesSettings: {
      argumentField: 'DAYMONTH',
      point: {
        visible: false
      },
    },
    series:
      [
        {
          type: 'line',
          valueField: 'PROPANE_CLOSING_INV_PERCENT',
          axis: 'PropaneGraph',
          name: 'Adjusted Inventory',
          color: COLORS.g_yellow,

        },

        }
      ]
    ,
    tooltip: {
      enabled: true,
      location: "edge",
      customizeTooltip: function (arg) {
        return {
          text: "Day: " + arg.argument + "<br/>" + arg.seriesName + ": " + Math.round(arg.valueText)
        };

  async function handleGenNom() {
    try {

      let ACTUAL_FROM_STOCK_PROJ_DATASOURCE = projectionGrid.option('dataSource');
      let Selected_month = nomMonthDropdown.option('selectedItem')?.toLowerCase();

        Selected_month: [{ Selected_month }],
        "WORKING_CAPACITY": [
          {
            "REGION": "EAST",
            "WORKING_CAPACITY_PROPANE": eastInputs?.working_capacity_propane?.option('value'),
            "WORKING_CAPACITY_BUTANE": eastInputs?.working_capacity_butane?.option('value')
          },
          {
            "REGION": "WEST",
            "WORKING_CAPACITY_PROPANE": westInputs?.working_capacity_propane?.option('value'),
            "WORKING_CAPACITY_BUTANE": westInputs?.working_capacity_butane?.option('value')
          }
        ],
        "ADJUSTED_CAPACITY": [
          {
            "REGION": "EAST",
            "ADJUSTED_CAPACITY_PROPANE": eastInputs?.adjust_capacity_propane?.option('value'),
            "ADJUSTED_CAPACITY_BUTANE": eastInputs?.adjust_capacity_butane?.option('value')
          },
          {

            "ADJUSTED_CAPACITY_PROPANE": westInputs?.adjust_capacity_propane?.option('value'),
            "ADJUSTED_CAPACITY_BUTANE": westInputs?.adjust_capacity_butane?.option('value')
          }
        ],
        "MIN": [
          {
            "REGION": "EAST",
            "MIN_BUTANE": eastInputs?.butane_min?.option('value'),
            "MIN_PROPANE": eastInputs?.propane_min?.option('value')
          },
          {
            "REGION": "WEST",
            "MIN_BUTANE": westInputs?.butane_min?.option('value'),
            "MIN_PROPANE": westInputs?.propane_min?.option('value')
          }
        ],
        "MAX": [
          {
            "REGION": "EAST",
            "MAX_BUTANE": eastInputs?.butane_max?.option('value'),
            "MAX_PROPANE": eastInputs?.propane_max?.option('value')
          },
          {
            "REGION": "WEST",
            "MAX_BUTANE": westInputs?.butane_max?.option('value'),
            "MAX_PROPANE": westInputs?.propane_max?.option('value')
          }
        ],
        ACTUAL_FROM_STOCK_PROJ: ACTUAL_FROM_STOCK_PROJ_DATASOURCE,
        ADJUSTMENT: dataSource
      };

      let finalJson = JSON.stringify({ DATA });
      let resp = await sendRequest(
        nominationSuggestionUrl,
        (method = "POST"),
        finalJson
      );
      showToast('success', 'Nomination Suggestion generated  successfully')
      let adjData = resp;

      handleUpdateAdjustGrid(adjData)


    } catch (error) {
      console.log('sugg error', error);
    }
  }

  async function sendRequest(url, method, data) {
    const d = $.Deferred();

    if (data === undefined) {
      data = "";
    }
    var myToken = await sasgetCSRFToken();

    $.ajax(url, {
      method,
      data,
      // xhrFields: { withCredentials: false },
      contentType: 'application/json',
      cache: false,
      // async: false,
      beforeSend: function (xhr) {
        xhr.setRequestHeader('X-CSRF-Token', myToken);
        xhr.setRequestHeader('X-CSRF-Header', 'X-CSRF-Token');
        $('.overlay').show();
      },
      complete: (xhr, status) => {
        $('.overlay').hide();
      }
    }).done((result) => {
      d.resolve(method === 'POST' ? result : result);
    }).fail((xhr) => {
      d.reject(xhr.responseJSON ? xhr.responseJSON.Message : xhr.statusText);
    });
    return d.promise();

  }

  async function sasgetCSRFToken() {
    const csrfURL = CSRF_URL
    const csrfParameters = { method: "GET", credentials: "include" }
    const csrfRequest = await fetch(csrfURL, csrfParameters)
    const csrfToken = await csrfRequest.headers.get("X-CSRF-TOKEN")
    return csrfToken
  }
});
